$CATEGORY: $course$ / Examples / Functions1

::Functions Level 1 #000::
What values are printed out at the end of the code?
<pre>void Absolute(int b, int a, int& c)
\{
	c = b + a % c;
\}
int main()
\{
	int list = 6;
	int foo = 10;
	int standings = 6;
	Absolute(list, foo, standings);
	cout << standings << endl;
	return 0;
\}</pre>	{
	=10
	~3.5
	~4
	~6
	~8
	}

::Functions Level 1 #001::
What values are printed out at the end of the code?
<pre>void Calculate(int a, int b, int c)
\{
	b = a / b % c;
\}
int main()
\{
	int item = 4;
	int list = 4;
	int dogs = 6;
	Calculate(item, list, dogs);
	cout << list << endl;
	return 0;
\}</pre>	{
	=4
	~2.5
	~3
	~6
	~1
	}

::Functions Level 1 #002::
What values are printed out at the end of the code?
<pre>void BinarySort(int& c, int& a, int b)
\{
	b = c + a / b;
\}
int main()
\{
	int foo = 10;
	int numbers = 8;
	int list = 8;
	BinarySort(foo, numbers, list);
	cout << list << endl;
	return 0;
\}</pre>	{
	=8
	~8.5
	~2.25
	~10
	~11
	}

::Functions Level 1 #003::

<pre>void Avg(int a, int c, int b)
\{
	b = a * c + b;
\}
int main()
\{
	int list = 2;
	int standings = 5;
	int documents = 7;
	Avg(list, standings, documents);
	cout << documents << endl;
	return 0;
\}</pre>	{
	=7
	~19.5
	~17
	~2
	~24
	}

::Functions Level 1 #005::

	b = a * b - c;
\}

	cout << standings << endl;
	return 0;
\}</pre>	{
	=1
	~1.5
	~0
	~10
	~-90
	}
